It is close to Taikoo Li on Chunxi Road, so it is very convenient for eating, drinking and having fun. When I arrived at the hotel on the day of check-in, I found that the hotel lobby was very similar to an express hotel chain. At that time, I wondered, why is a five-star hotel so shabby? When consulting at the front desk, the front desk clerk told me that this hotel was a "Five Diamond" and not a "Five Star". At that time, I felt that I had been cheated. Is there still a "How many diamonds" in hotel ratings now? What's even more frustrating is that the room I booked has no windows. My colleagues and I have been arguing with the front desk, why does the room costing more than 700 yuan a night have no windows? The waiter said very rudely, take a closer look at the Ctrip booking page to see if there are windows! Firm attitude and sharp tone. My colleague was very angry and asked if he could speak properly. The front desk clerk said, then you should find another hotel to check into. At this time we were stunned. I travel for business all year round and often stay in hotels. This is the first time I have seen a waiter like this. He can't help but explain the service. Because it was already getting late, my colleagues and I went out at 6 a.m. and checked into the hotel at around 6 p.m. We were already exhausted and didn‚Äôt want to bother, so we compromised and said we would stay in the hotel for one day and then change. I returned to the hotel very late and still stayed in the original room. We booked for 4 days and have already stayed for 2 days. We don‚Äôt want to change hotels. The front desk finally got nice and said that they could change rooms tomorrow. But we need to cancel the room we booked on Ctrip for 2 days left, and the hotel will help us change it. Another tossing. On the morning of check-out, after breakfast, when we went to the room to pick up our luggage and prepare to check out, another thrilling scene happened. Breakfast is on the 9th floor. The hotel's breakfast is very average, just like the breakfast at an express hotel. After breakfast, when we took the elevator to the 20th floor, the elevator suddenly dropped. We were shocked. The power supply and display screen in the elevator instantly went black. Shaking. I pressed the emergency call button desperately, but to no avail. About a minute later, the elevator door suddenly opened. The distance between the elevator and the floor was about 20 centimeters. Unexpectedly, the hotel waiter told us that they knew there was a problem with the elevator and were arranging maintenance personnel to come and take a look. We are completely speechless.
